ago","","An exceptional hotel that thoroughly deserves every award it receives\n\nSpending a blissful 11 nights here as a family of 4. That Hotel Royal Ambarrukmo stays true to its 5* billing goes without saying- it's elegant, luxurious, the hotel and the adjacent buildings have a great backstory that add to their charm- but what really sets Royal Ambarrukmo apart is the high level of service and attention to detail from its hardworking, dedicated staff and guest relations (Heru, Guest Relations Manager, warrants a special mention here). Despite our stay coinciding with a high profile event attended by senior military figures, the staff went to great lengths to ensure we felt special- within a day of arrival everyone from reception to restaurant staff knew the kids by their names, our breakfast choices were noted and served subsequently without being requested, they were willing to reallocate staff to accommodate even our smallest request, every staff we met greeted us with a smile, followed by ' is there anything else I can do to assist you'? The fact they approach a 'regular' guest with such care and attention suggests this is part of the hotel's corporate culture and ethos and is a huge credit to the management and staff here.\n\nThe facilities at the hotel have been discussed to death in other reviews so don't bear repeating- I'd only add that the staff work tirelessly to keep the place spotless. The added attraction is that Indonesians do not appear to be big fans of the swimming pool after 10 am so you are more or less guaranteed exclusive use of it between 10-6 pm. The same goes for the well equipped fitness centre and sauna, both of which I've had to myself every time I've used it, regardless of the hour and occupancy of the hotel. Breakfast is sumptuous and varied, with plenty of live food counters serving local and continental cuisine and tends to remain open beyond the official hours of 6:30-10 am. The Kids Club is staffed based on demand but my kids have used it lot and absolutely adore Michelle, one of the staff members. It also contains a lot of very expensive kit such as PS 5s, VR headsets, several desktops etc that are guaranteed to appeal to kids of all ages.\n\nThe city centre location may not be to everyone's liking but from our perspective, proximity to Ambarrukmo Plaza with it's excellent selection of shops and restaurants is a huge advantage. As for room layout, city facing rooms overlook a busy road and can be noisier than garden facing ones so light sleepers may want to request the latter.\n\nMy family spent last Xmas in one of the most exclusive hotels in Jumeirah, Dubai and, based purely on service, rate this place higher than the former. Though it's an excruciating flight halfway across the world, Royal Ambarrukmo has been so good we are almost tempted to return to Yogya for a holiday just so we can stay here again!\nHighly recommended.",5,"","107588835352789007878",["https://www.google.com/local/review/rap/report?postId\u003dChZDSUhNMG9nS0VJQ0FnSUN1aWRHQ0lnEAE\u0026entityid\u003dChZDSUhNMG9nS0VJQ0FnSUN1aWRHQ0lnEi4KF0NJSE0wb2dLRUlDQWdJQ3VpZEdDb2dFEhNDZ3dJMnV5Wmx3WVEtS1h0MVFNGi0KFkNJSE0wb2dLRUlDQWdJQ3VpZEdDWWcSE0Nnd0kydXlabHdZUS1LWHQxUU0iEgn5xYMl6Fl6LhHy7qSWwr_sjSoTQ2d3STJ1eVpsd1lRLUtYdDFRTQ\u0026wv\u003d1\u0026d\u003d286732320","Flag
